# Brick element for linear 3d elasticity 

## Nomenclature 

### Coordinates of the current point 

``` 
[x , x , x ] 
  1   2   3
``` 

### Dimensions of the element 

``` 
[h , h , h ] 
  1   2   3
``` 

### Numbering of nodes 

``` 
node        = [x  = 0, x  = 0, x  = 0] 
    1, 1, 1     1       2       3

node        = [x  = 0, x  = 0, x  = h ] 
    1, 1, 2     1       2       3    3

node        = [x  = 0, x  = h , x  = 0] 
    1, 2, 1     1       2    2   3

node        = [x  = 0, x  = h , x  = h ] 
    1, 2, 2     1       2    2   3    3

node        = [x  = h , x  = 0, x  = 0] 
    2, 1, 1     1    1   2       3

node        = [x  = h , x  = 0, x  = h ] 
    2, 1, 2     1    1   2       3    3

node        = [x  = h , x  = h , x  = 0] 
    2, 2, 1     1    1   2    2   3

node        = [x  = h , x  = h , x  = h ] 
    2, 2, 2     1    1   2    2   3    3

``` 

## Shape functions and interpolation of the displacements 

``` 
                x        x        x
                 1        2        3
N        = (1 - --) (1 - --) (1 - --) 
 1, 1, 1        h        h        h
                 1        2        3

                x        x
                 1        2
           (1 - --) (1 - --) x
                h        h    3
                 1        2
N        = -------------------- 
 1, 1, 2            h
                     3

                x           x
                 1           3
           (1 - --) x  (1 - --)
                h    2      h
                 1           3
N        = -------------------- 
 1, 2, 1            h
                     2

                x
                 1
           (1 - --) x  x
                h    2  3
                 1
N        = -------------- 
 1, 2, 2       h  h
                2  3

                   x        x
                    2        3
           x  (1 - --) (1 - --)
            1      h        h
                    2        3
N        = -------------------- 
 2, 1, 1            h
                     1

                   x
                    2
           x  (1 - --) x
            1      h    3
                    2
N        = -------------- 
 2, 1, 2       h  h
                1  3

                      x
                       3
           x  x  (1 - --)
            1  2      h
                       3
N        = -------------- 
 2, 2, 1       h  h
                1  2

           x  x  x
            1  2  3
N        = -------- 
 2, 2, 2   h  h  h
            1  2  3

``` 

Testing numbering of vertices... 
... OK 

Testing that interpolated displacements are correct at vertices... 
... OK 

We get the following expressions for the displacements 

``` 
u  = xi  xi  xi  u             + xi  xi  (1 - xi ) u             + xi  (1 - xi ) xi  u
 1     1   2   3  [2, 2, 2], 1     1   2        3   [2, 2, 1], 1     1        2    3  [2, 1, 2], 1
 + xi  (1 - xi ) (1 - xi ) u             + (1 - xi ) xi  xi  u             + (1 - xi ) xi  (1 - xi ) u
     1        2         3   [2, 1, 1], 1          1    2   3  [1, 2, 2], 1          1    2        3   [1, 2, 1], 1
 + (1 - xi ) (1 - xi ) xi  u             + (1 - xi ) (1 - xi ) (1 - xi ) u             
          1         2    3  [1, 1, 2], 1          1         2         3   [1, 1, 1], 1

u  = xi  xi  xi  u             + xi  xi  (1 - xi ) u             + xi  (1 - xi ) xi  u
 2     1   2   3  [2, 2, 2], 2     1   2        3   [2, 2, 1], 2     1        2    3  [2, 1, 2], 2
 + xi  (1 - xi ) (1 - xi ) u             + (1 - xi ) xi  xi  u             + (1 - xi ) xi  (1 - xi ) u
     1        2         3   [2, 1, 1], 2          1    2   3  [1, 2, 2], 2          1    2        3   [1, 2, 1], 2
 + (1 - xi ) (1 - xi ) xi  u             + (1 - xi ) (1 - xi ) (1 - xi ) u             
          1         2    3  [1, 1, 2], 2          1         2         3   [1, 1, 1], 2

u  = xi  xi  xi  u             + xi  xi  (1 - xi ) u             + xi  (1 - xi ) xi  u
 3     1   2   3  [2, 2, 2], 3     1   2        3   [2, 2, 1], 3     1        2    3  [2, 1, 2], 3
 + xi  (1 - xi ) (1 - xi ) u             + (1 - xi ) xi  xi  u             + (1 - xi ) xi  (1 - xi ) u
     1        2         3   [2, 1, 1], 3          1    2   3  [1, 2, 2], 3          1    2        3   [1, 2, 1], 3
 + (1 - xi ) (1 - xi ) xi  u             + (1 - xi ) (1 - xi ) (1 - xi ) u             
          1         2    3  [1, 1, 2], 3          1         2         3   [1, 1, 1], 3

```

## Stiffness matrix 

Testing that elastic energy is retrieved from extracted stiffness matrix... 
... OK 
We get the following coefficients of the stiffness operator 

``` 
                              4 h  h  mu   2 h  h  mu   2 h  h  mu   2 h  h  lambda_
                                 2  3         1  3         1  2         2  3
K                           = ---------- + ---------- + ---------- + --------------- 
 [1, 1, 1], 1, [1, 1, 1], 1      9 h          9 h          9 h            9 h
                                    1            2            3              1

                              h  mu   h  lambda_
                               3       3
K                           = ----- + ---------- 
 [1, 1, 1], 1, [1, 1, 1], 2     6         6

                              h  mu   h  lambda_
                               2       2
K                           = ----- + ---------- 
 [1, 1, 1], 1, [1, 1, 1], 3     6         6

                              2 h  h  mu   h  h  mu   2 h  h  mu   h  h  lambda_
                                 2  3       1  3         1  2       2  3
K                           = ---------- + -------- - ---------- + ------------- 
 [1, 1, 1], 1, [1, 1, 2], 1      9 h         9 h         9 h           9 h
                                    1           2           3             1

                              h  mu   h  lambda_
                               3       3
K                           = ----- + ---------- 
 [1, 1, 1], 1, [1, 1, 2], 2    12         12

                              h  mu   h  lambda_
                               2       2
K                           = ----- - ---------- 
 [1, 1, 1], 1, [1, 1, 2], 3     6         6

                              2 h  h  mu   2 h  h  mu   h  h  mu   h  h  lambda_
                                 2  3         1  3       1  2       2  3
K                           = ---------- - ---------- + -------- + ------------- 
 [1, 1, 1], 1, [1, 2, 1], 1      9 h          9 h         9 h          9 h
                                    1            2           3            1

                              h  mu   h  lambda_
                               3       3
K                           = ----- - ---------- 
 [1, 1, 1], 1, [1, 2, 1], 2     6         6

                              h  mu   h  lambda_
                               2       2
K                           = ----- + ---------- 
 [1, 1, 1], 1, [1, 2, 1], 3    12         12

                              h  h  mu   h  h  mu   h  h  mu   h  h  lambda_
``` 
